<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="East_and_North">East and North</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_and_the_Humber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: East and North">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="box-More_citations_needed_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_and_the_Humber&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.<br /><small><span class="plainlinks"><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22">"Yorkshire and the Humber"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbm=nws&amp;q=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22+-wikipedia">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?&amp;q=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22+site:news.google.com/newspapers&amp;source=newspapers">newspapers</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22+-wikipedia">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Yorkshire+and+the+Humber%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a></span></small></span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">November 2016</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_(geograph_508425).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_%28geograph_508425%29.jpg/220px-Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_%28geograph_508425%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="337" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_%28geograph_508425%29.jpg/330px-Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_%28geograph_508425%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e1/Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_%28geograph_508425%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="418" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Corus_automated_mill_in_construction_(geograph_508425).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>British Steel Limited <a href="/wiki/Scunthorpe_Steelworks" title="Scunthorpe Steelworks">steelworks at Scunthorpe</a></div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_steel_production" title="List of countries by steel production">List of countries by steel production</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Scunthorpe" title="Scunthorpe">Scunthorpe</a> is where steel is <a href="/wiki/Smelting" title="Smelting">smelted</a> by <a href="/wiki/British_Steel_Limited" title="British Steel Limited">British Steel Limited</a> (former Corus Group before September 2010 then <a href="/wiki/Tata_Steel_Europe" title="Tata Steel Europe">Tata Steel Europe</a> until June 2016) in the east of the town; it is the largest steelworks in the UK. <a href="/wiki/Golden_Wonder" title="Golden Wonder">Golden Wonder</a> crisps are made in <a href="/wiki/Frodingham,_Lincolnshire" title="Frodingham, Lincolnshire">Frodingham</a>, opposite the steel works (former site of Riley's Potato Crisps); the brand originated in Scotland. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Esca_Food_Solutions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Esca Food Solutions (page does not exist)">Esca Food Solutions</a> (another plant was in <a href="/wiki/Milton_Keynes" title="Milton Keynes">Milton Keynes</a> before October 2007) make all the beef <a href="/wiki/Patty" title="Patty">patties</a> for <a href="/wiki/McDonald%27s" title="McDonald&#39;s">McDonald's</a> in the UK and Ireland at their factory in <a href="/wiki/Crosby,_Lincolnshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Crosby, Lincolnshire">Crosby</a> in the north-west of the town, processing around 7000 cattle a week – about 12,000&#160;kg an hour; 2.25m cattle are killed in the UK each year. <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_Automotive_Components&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International Automotive Components (page does not exist)">IAC Group</a> (Ecomold before 2008) have a car interiors plant on the Foxhills Ind Est in the north of Scunthorpe off the A1077; to the west, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Can-Pack&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Can-Pack (page does not exist)">Can-Pack</a> UK (parent company in <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Kraków">Kraków</a>) is on the Skippingdale Ind Est, and makes alumninium <a href="/wiki/Beverage_can" class="mw-redirect" title="Beverage can">beverage cans</a>; further north, <a href="/wiki/Nisa_(retailer)" title="Nisa (retailer)">Nisa</a> (retailer) have their headquarters on the <a href="/wiki/Normanby,_North_Lincolnshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Normanby, North Lincolnshire">Normanby</a> Enterprise Park, in <a href="/wiki/Flixborough" title="Flixborough">Flixborough</a> off the B1430. Further south on the Foxhills Ind Est towards the <a href="/wiki/A1077_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A1077 road">A1077</a>, Wren Kitchens have a large factory in a former <a href="/wiki/B%26Q" title="B&amp;Q">B&amp;Q</a> warehouse, which closed in 2009; next-door to the north, <a href="/wiki/2_Sisters_Food_Group" title="2 Sisters Food Group">2 Sisters Food Group</a> have a large chicken processing plant (Premier Fresh Foods before 2000), built in 1988 as one of the largest plants of its type in Europe, which processes around 1,900,000 chickens per week (370 chickens per minute, and customers include <a href="/wiki/KFC" title="KFC">KFC</a>). TSC Foods on the Queensway Ind Estate at the <a href="/wiki/A18_road_(England)" title="A18 road (England)">A18</a>/A1029 roundabout in south-east Scunthorpe supply many foodservice products (sauces) to most UK <a href="/wiki/Pub_chain" title="Pub chain">pub chains</a>. Caparo Merchant Bar, next to the steel works in Scunthorpe, are the UK's largest producer of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Merchant_bar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Merchant bar (page does not exist)">merchant bar</a>; nearby is British Steel Wire Rod. Vossloh Cogifer UK (former Corus Cogifer before 2012), a joint venture of <a href="/wiki/Vossloh" title="Vossloh">Vossloh Cogifer</a> (of <a href="/wiki/Reichshoffen" title="Reichshoffen">Reichshoffen</a>) and the former Corus Rail, make <a href="/wiki/Railroad_switch" title="Railroad switch">railway points</a> to the west of Scunthorpe; <a href="/wiki/Voestalpine" title="Voestalpine">Voestalpine</a> also make train tracks too at a huge foundry in Austria
</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pipers_Crisps&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Pipers Crisps (page does not exist)">Pipers Crisps</a> are on a <a href="/wiki/RAF_Elsham_Wolds" title="RAF Elsham Wolds">former airfield</a> next to the A15 at <a href="/wiki/Elsham,_North_Lincolnshire" title="Elsham, North Lincolnshire">Elsham</a>; next door is IG Industries who produce polyethylene films (<a href="/wiki/Shrink_wrap" title="Shrink wrap">shrink wrap</a>). There are two large oil refineries west of <a href="/wiki/Immingham" title="Immingham">Immingham</a>, owned by <a href="/wiki/ConocoPhillips" title="ConocoPhillips">ConocoPhillips</a> (<a href="/wiki/Jet_(brand)" title="Jet (brand)">Jet</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Total_S.A." title="Total S.A.">Total</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kimberly-Clark" title="Kimberly-Clark">Kimberly-Clark</a> made all of its <i><a href="/wiki/Huggies" title="Huggies">Huggies</a></i> nappies for Europe at <a href="/wiki/Barton-upon-Humber" title="Barton-upon-Humber">Barton-upon-Humber</a> until 2013; since 2016, the site has been the headquarters and factory of <a href="/wiki/Wren_Kitchens" title="Wren Kitchens">Wren Kitchens</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Techrete&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Techrete (page does not exist)">Techrete</a> on the B1207 in the north of Hibaldstow, next to the <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_to_Lincoln_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Sheffield to Lincoln Line">railway line</a>, is the UK's leading maker of architectural precast <a href="/wiki/Cladding_(construction)" title="Cladding (construction)">cladding</a>. County Turf, off the B1207 (Ermine Street) in <a href="/wiki/Appleby,_North_Lincolnshire" title="Appleby, North Lincolnshire">Appleby</a> made the turf for <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>, who replaced Inturf of <a href="/wiki/Wilberfoss" title="Wilberfoss">Wilberfoss</a>. There is a large <a href="/wiki/Cemex" title="Cemex">CEMEX</a> <a href="/wiki/Cement" title="Cement">cement</a> plant at <a href="/wiki/Winteringham" title="Winteringham">Winteringham</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A1077_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A1077 road">A1077</a> at the meeting point of the New <a href="/wiki/River_Ancholme" title="River Ancholme">River Ancholme</a> and the Humber (<a href="/wiki/Ferriby_Sluice" title="Ferriby Sluice">Ferriby Sluice</a>).
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Industry_of_the_South_Humber_Bank" title="Industry of the South Humber Bank">Industry of the South Humber Bank</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Woad_Lane_(geograph_2124433).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg/220px-Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg/330px-Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg/440px-Woad_Lane_%28geograph_2124433%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Woad_Lane_(geograph_2124433).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The 226-acre <a href="/wiki/Novartis" title="Novartis">Novartis</a> Grimsby in Great Coates, next to the Europarc in the west of Grimsby; it has been there since 1951, firstly as Ciba (Chemical Industry Basel) making <a href="/wiki/Sulfathiazole" title="Sulfathiazole">sulfathiazole</a></div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Grimsby" title="Grimsby">Grimsby</a> is home of England's <a href="/wiki/Fishing_industry_in_England" title="Fishing industry in England">fishing industry</a> (although most fish is transported from the <a href="/wiki/Peterhead" title="Peterhead">Peterhead</a> area of Scotland via road), and has many frozen food factories such as <a href="/wiki/Young%27s_Seafood" title="Young&#39;s Seafood">Young's Seafood</a>. The seafood industry is worth £1.8&#160;billion to North East Lincolnshire; most of Britain's seafood comes from Grimsby. <a href="/wiki/HM_Revenue_%26_Customs" class="mw-redirect" title="HM Revenue &amp; Customs">HM Revenue &amp; Customs</a> in the town centre administers the UK's deregistration of <a href="/wiki/Value-added_tax_(United_Kingdom)" class="mw-redirect" title="Value-added tax (United Kingdom)">VAT</a> for companies, and the VAT Annual Accounting Scheme. <a href="/wiki/Auto-Trail" title="Auto-Trail">Auto-Trail</a> makes motorhomes on the <a href="/wiki/Europarc,_Grimsby" class="mw-redirect" title="Europarc, Grimsby">Europarc, Grimsby</a>, owned by Paris-based <a href="/w/index.php?title=Trigano&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Trigano (page does not exist)">Trigano</a>. Wyndeham Gait is a main printer next to the <a href="/wiki/A180_road_(England)" title="A180 road (England)">A180</a>/<a href="/wiki/A16_road_(England)" title="A16 road (England)">A16</a> roundabout. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Icelandic_Seachill&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Icelandic Seachill (page does not exist)">Icelandic Seachill</a>, south of the A180 Pyewipe Roundabout, makes McDonald's <a href="/wiki/Filet-O-Fish" title="Filet-O-Fish">Filet-O-Fish</a>. <a href="/wiki/Cardsave" title="Cardsave">Cardsave</a> is a <a href="/wiki/Merchant_account_provider" title="Merchant account provider">merchant account provider</a>. Cofely Fabricom <a href="/wiki/Engie" title="Engie">Engie</a> (former GDF SUEZ), an engineering consultancy based on the A1173 in Immingham, work in the oil and gas industry, and nearby to the east is a large <a href="/wiki/Knauf" title="Knauf">Knauf</a> plaster board plant. <a href="/wiki/Norsk_Hydro" title="Norsk Hydro">Hydro Agri</a> had an important large fertiliser plant (built by <a href="/wiki/Fisons" title="Fisons">Fisons</a> in 1951) on the side of the railway; now <a href="/w/index.php?title=PB_Kent&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="PB Kent (page does not exist)">PB Kent</a> and its subsidiary <a href="/w/index.php?title=Humber_Palmers&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Humber Palmers (page does not exist)">Humber Palmers</a> (both owned by <a href="/wiki/Origin_Enterprises" title="Origin Enterprises">Origin Enterprises</a> of Ireland) make fertiliser there. In Healing (former <a href="/wiki/Little_Coates" title="Little Coates">Little Coates</a>) next to the Humber, <a href="/wiki/Lenzing_AG" title="Lenzing AG">Lenzing Fibers Grimsby</a> make <a href="/wiki/Lyocell" title="Lyocell">Lyocell</a> (Tencel), where it was first made by Courtaulds in 1988, who owned the site until bought by <a href="/wiki/AkzoNobel" title="AkzoNobel">AkzoNobel</a> in 1998; next door is BASF Performance Products (former Ciba). Nearby to south off the A1136/A180 junction is <a href="/wiki/Europarc,_Grimsby" class="mw-redirect" title="Europarc, Grimsby">Europarc</a>, also in Healing, where <a href="/wiki/Kerry_Group" title="Kerry Group">Kerry Group</a> mothballed its frozen food factory in 2012; further to east in the former Little Coates is Novartis, Dunlop Oil &amp; Marine (owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Contitech&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Contitech (page does not exist)">Contitech</a>, who make rubber <a href="/wiki/Hose" title="Hose">hose</a>). <a href="/wiki/Greenergy" title="Greenergy">Greenergy</a> have a biodiesel plant at <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Immingham" title="Port of Immingham">Immingham West Terminal</a>. Grimsby imports around 500,000 vehicles a year. The area's ports take 15% of Britain's <a href="/wiki/Roll-on/roll-off" title="Roll-on/roll-off">ro-ro</a> cargo; only Dover takes more.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Rank_Ltd.,_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Joseph_Rank_Ltd.%2C_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg/220px-Joseph_Rank_Ltd.%2C_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="327" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Joseph_Rank_Ltd.%2C_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg/330px-Joseph_Rank_Ltd.%2C_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/81/Joseph_Rank_Ltd.%2C_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg 2x" data-file-width="431" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Rank_Ltd.,_Hull_-_geograph.org.uk_-_664662.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Joseph Rank Ltd in Hull in January 2008</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/AarhusKarlshamn" class="mw-redirect" title="AarhusKarlshamn">AarhusKarlshamn</a> UK (AAK, <a href="/wiki/Cooking_oil" title="Cooking oil">edible oils</a>) is at Hull Ferry Terminal. The <a href="/wiki/Valuation_Office_Agency" title="Valuation Office Agency">Valuation Office Agency</a> for the north of England is near King George Dock. <a href="/wiki/Smith_%26_Nephew" title="Smith &amp; Nephew">Smith &amp; Nephew</a> (wound management division) and <a href="/wiki/Reckitt_Benckiser" title="Reckitt Benckiser">Reckitt Benckiser</a> medical and household products companies originated in Hull, and still have large factories there. When <a href="/wiki/Reckitt_%26_Colman" class="mw-redirect" title="Reckitt &amp; Colman">Reckitt &amp; Colman</a> merged with the Dutch Benckiser in 1999, much production was moved from Hull to <a href="/wiki/Swindon" title="Swindon">Swindon</a>. <a href="/wiki/Heron_Foods" title="Heron Foods">Heron Frozen Foods</a> is based there near St Andrew's Quay, and <a href="/wiki/Cranswick_plc" title="Cranswick plc">Cranswick plc</a> are a food-processing company based in the north of Hull, which makes up-market (<i>Taste the Difference</i>) <a href="/wiki/Gourmet" title="Gourmet">gourmet</a> sausages for Tesco and <a href="/wiki/Sainsbury%27s" title="Sainsbury&#39;s">Sainsbury's</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wilfred_Emmanuel-Jones" title="Wilfred Emmanuel-Jones">The Black Farmer</a>, in West Carr; Cranswick Country Foods have their main <a href="/wiki/Poultry_farming" title="Poultry farming">poultry processing</a> site off the B1237 in the north of <a href="/wiki/Stoneferry" title="Stoneferry">Stoneferry</a>; nearby to the north is <a href="/wiki/Greencore" title="Greencore">Greencore</a> Grocery (<a href="/wiki/Birthday_cake" title="Birthday cake">birthday cakes</a> &amp; desserts). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maizecor&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Maizecor (page does not exist)">Maizecor</a> (<a href="/wiki/Maize" title="Maize">maize</a>) are in Wincolmlee. Croda Europe has a chemical factory on the north side of the <a href="/wiki/A1165_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A1165 road">A1165</a> in <a href="/wiki/Newland,_East_Riding_of_Yorkshire" title="Newland, East Riding of Yorkshire">Newland</a> next to River Hull; further south in <a href="/wiki/Sculcoates" title="Sculcoates">Sculcoates</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crown_Paints" title="Crown Paints">Crown Paints</a> have a factory on the west side of the River Hull. Walker Group in Hull own Victoria Plumb bathrooms, and the brand <a href="/wiki/MFI_Group" title="MFI Group">MFI</a>. <a href="/wiki/Aunt_Bessie%27s" title="Aunt Bessie&#39;s">Aunt Bessie's</a> is a large food company in the west of Hull near the <a href="/wiki/A63_road" title="A63 road">A63</a> and Hessle. Nearby <a href="/wiki/Norbert_Dentressangle" title="Norbert Dentressangle">Norbert Dentressangle</a> claim to run the largest <a href="/wiki/Pea" title="Pea">pea</a> processing factory in the world<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> at the junction of the A1166 and the <i>Clive Sullivan Way</i> (A63), which has supplied all of <a href="/wiki/Birds_Eye" title="Birds Eye">Birds Eye</a>'s peas since June 2008.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ideal_Standard" title="Ideal Standard">Ideal Standard</a>, the plumbing company, now in north Hull next to the <a href="/wiki/Hull%E2%80%93Scarborough_line" title="Hull–Scarborough line">Hull–Scarborough line</a> (Yorkshire Coast Line), was formed in Hull in 1936. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ideal_Heating&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ideal Heating (page does not exist)">Ideal Heating</a>, owned by <a href="/wiki/Stelrad" title="Stelrad">Stelrad</a> and based nearby, make <a href="/wiki/Water_heating" title="Water heating">domestic boilers</a>, and have diversified into <a href="/wiki/Air_source_heat_pumps" title="Air source heat pumps">air source heat pumps</a> and <a href="/wiki/Solar_thermal_collector" title="Solar thermal collector">solar thermal</a> water heaters. <a href="/wiki/Comet_Group" title="Comet Group">Comet</a>, who originated there, had some main offices on <i>George Street</i>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gamebore_Cartridge&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gamebore Cartridge (page does not exist)">Gamebore Cartridge</a> on the A1165 at <a href="/wiki/Drypool" title="Drypool">Drypool</a>, Hull and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hull_Cartridge&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hull Cartridge (page does not exist)">Hull Cartridge</a>, on the Acorn Ind Estate north of Ideal, both make <a href="/wiki/Shotgun_shell" title="Shotgun shell">shotgun cartridges</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Logan_Teleflex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Logan Teleflex (page does not exist)">Logan Teleflex</a> (former Fabricom Airport Systems, and owned by Daifuku) makes luggage sorting systems near the B1237/A1033 junction in north Hull. <a href="/wiki/KCOM_Group" title="KCOM Group">KCOM Group</a> (former Kingston Communications) is an iconic<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (August 2018)">clarification needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> telecommunications company based next to <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_Hall" title="Hull City Hall">Hull City Hall</a>. <a href="/wiki/Seven_Seas_(company)" title="Seven Seas (company)">Seven Seas</a>, owned by <a href="/wiki/Merck_Group" title="Merck Group">Merck Group</a>, made <a href="/wiki/Cod_liver_oil" title="Cod liver oil">cod liver oil</a> and <a href="/wiki/Multivitamin" title="Multivitamin">multivitamins</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=Haliborange&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Haliborange (page does not exist)">Haliborange</a>) on the <a href="/wiki/A1033_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A1033 road">A1033</a> in <a href="/wiki/Marfleet" title="Marfleet">Marfleet</a> until 2015; next door is Willerby Holiday Homes, the UK's largest manufacturer of holiday homes; nearby, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Paneltex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Paneltex (page does not exist)">Paneltex</a> is a group of engineering companies for vehicle bodies, on the Kingston International Park on the A1033, opposite Saltend; next door is Atlas Leisure Homes (in Preston). Humdinger (owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Zetar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Zetar (page does not exist)">Zetar</a>) on the A1033 makes branded savoury snacks. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Airbath&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Airbath (page does not exist)">Airbath</a> (part of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Reva_Industries&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reva Industries (page does not exist)">Reva Industries</a>) is in north-east Hull. <a href="/wiki/Dunlop_(brands)" title="Dunlop (brands)">Fenner Dunlop</a> Europe who claim to be the world's largest <a href="/wiki/Conveyor_belt" title="Conveyor belt">conveyor belt</a> manufacturer, in Marfleet, have their own <a href="/wiki/Cricket_pitch" title="Cricket pitch">cricket pitch</a> and their <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hainsworth_Research_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hainsworth Research Centre (page does not exist)">Hainsworth Research Centre</a>.
</p><p>BP Saltend (in <a href="/wiki/Preston,_East_Riding_of_Yorkshire" title="Preston, East Riding of Yorkshire">Preston</a>) is Europe's largest producer of <a href="/wiki/Acetic_acid" title="Acetic acid">acetic acid</a>, and part of the worldwide BP <a href="/wiki/Acetyl" class="mw-redirect" title="Acetyl">Acetyls</a> group; next door, <a href="/wiki/Ineos" title="Ineos">Ineos</a> Enterprises makes <a href="/wiki/Vinyl_acetate" title="Vinyl acetate">vinyl acetate monomer</a> (VAM) and <a href="/wiki/Vivergo" class="mw-redirect" title="Vivergo">Vivergo</a> (bioethanol) is nearby. <a href="/wiki/Fenner_PLC" title="Fenner PLC">Fenner PLC</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Hessle" title="Hessle">Hessle</a>. <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Military_Air_%26_Information" title="BAE Systems Military Air &amp; Information">BAE Systems Military Air &amp; Information</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Blackburn_Aircraft" title="Blackburn Aircraft">Blackburn Aircraft</a>, and under threat of imminent closure) at <a href="/wiki/Brough,_East_Riding_of_Yorkshire" title="Brough, East Riding of Yorkshire">Brough</a> is known as the <i>Home of the Hawk</i>, and recently made the <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Hawk" title="BAE Systems Hawk">Hawk 128</a>, with a fully <a href="/wiki/Glass_cockpit" title="Glass cockpit">digital cockpit</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kohler_Mira_Ltd" class="mw-redirect" title="Kohler Mira Ltd">Kohler Mira Ltd</a> make showers on the Melton West Business Park, south of the A63. <a href="/wiki/Guardian_Industries" title="Guardian Industries">Guardian Industries</a> makes <a href="/wiki/Float_glass" title="Float glass">float glass</a> in <a href="/wiki/Goole" title="Goole">Goole</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Baracuta_Clothing&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Baracuta Clothing (page does not exist)">Baracuta Clothing</a>, off A614/A161 junction on the Grange Park Ind Estate are owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Baird_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Baird Group (page does not exist)">Baird Group</a> (former William Baird) of Leeds off Granary Wharf next to Bridgewater Place, which also owns the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Racing_Green_(clothing)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Racing Green (clothing) (page does not exist)">Racing Green</a> brand. Timloc, part of <a href="/wiki/Alumasc_Group" title="Alumasc Group">Alumasc Group</a>, make ventilation for buildings. <a href="/wiki/Croda_International" title="Croda International">Croda International</a>, the chemical company, is in <a href="/wiki/East_Cowick" title="East Cowick">East Cowick</a>, near the M62/M18 Langham Interchange. <a href="/wiki/Swift_Leisure" title="Swift Leisure">Swift Group</a> in Cottingham are the only UK manufacturer of caravans. <a href="/wiki/Yara_International" title="Yara International">Yara</a> UK have a fertiliser blending plant (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=Phosyn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Phosyn (page does not exist)">Phosyn</a> before 2006) on the A1079 on a former <a href="/wiki/RAF_Pocklington" title="RAF Pocklington">airfield</a> in <a href="/wiki/Barmby_Moor" title="Barmby Moor">Barmby Moor</a>. Bridlington is Europe's largest <a href="/wiki/Lobster_fishing" title="Lobster fishing">lobster port</a>.
</p><p>There are many <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> bases in <a href="/wiki/North_Yorkshire" title="North Yorkshire">North Yorkshire</a>, close to the A1, <a href="/wiki/Catterick_Garrison" title="Catterick Garrison">Catterick Garrison</a> is the largest army base in Europe near <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_North_Yorkshire" title="Richmond, North Yorkshire">Richmond</a>, and home of the <a href="/wiki/Infantry_Training_Centre_(British_Army)" title="Infantry Training Centre (British Army)">Infantry Training Centre</a>. The <a href="/wiki/RAF_Leconfield" title="RAF Leconfield">Defence School of Transport Leconfield</a> is near <a href="/wiki/Beverley" title="Beverley">Beverley</a>. <a href="/wiki/RAF_Fylingdales" title="RAF Fylingdales">RAF Fylingdales</a> is an important, though secret, part of NATO's <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_Missile_Early_Warning_System" title="Ballistic Missile Early Warning System">Ballistic Missile Early Warning System</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Planning_College" title="Emergency Planning College">Emergency Planning College</a> at <a href="/wiki/Easingwold" title="Easingwold">Easingwold</a> provided courses to prepare for <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_warfare" title="Nuclear warfare">nuclear war</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dishforth_Airfield" title="Dishforth Airfield">Dishforth Airfield</a> was the first place in the UK to get the Apache helicopter in 2003 for the <a href="/wiki/Army_Air_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="Army Air Corps (United Kingdom)">Army Air Corps</a>, and has had helicopters since 1991, currently having three squadrons of <a href="/wiki/Westland_Lynx" title="Westland Lynx">Lynx</a> helicopters. The helicopters train over the North York Moors. <a href="/wiki/4th_Regiment_Royal_Artillery" title="4th Regiment Royal Artillery">4th Regiment Royal Artillery</a> is at <a href="/wiki/Alanbrooke_Barracks" title="Alanbrooke Barracks">Alanbrooke Barracks</a> (former RAF Topcliffe, and former HQ of <a href="/wiki/15th_Infantry_Brigade_(United_Kingdom)" title="15th Infantry Brigade (United Kingdom)">15th Infantry Brigade</a>, which is now at <a href="/wiki/Imphal_Barracks" title="Imphal Barracks">Imphal Barracks</a>). GCHQ (former Composite Signals Organisation) have a <a href="/wiki/GCHQ_Scarborough" title="GCHQ Scarborough">site</a> in the west of Scarborough. <a href="/wiki/RAF_Leeming" title="RAF Leeming">RAF Leeming</a> is the only RAF station in <a href="/wiki/Northern_England" title="Northern England">Northern England</a> that flies jet aircraft; the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Universities_Air_Squadron" title="Yorkshire Universities Air Squadron">Yorkshire Universities Air Squadron</a> flies from <a href="/wiki/RAF_Linton-on-Ouse" title="RAF Linton-on-Ouse">RAF Linton-on-Ouse</a> (previously it had flown from <a href="/wiki/RAF_Church_Fenton" title="RAF Church Fenton">RAF Church Fenton</a> until 2013).<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestlé">Nestlé</a> in the UK are based in York, with <a href="/wiki/Mackintosh%27s" title="Mackintosh&#39;s">Mackintosh's</a> operations in Halifax. <a href="/wiki/Persimmon_plc" title="Persimmon plc">Persimmon plc</a> (the UK's second largest builder of houses, building around 14,000 houses in 2014) is at the A19/A64 Fulford Interchange. The <a href="/wiki/Shepherd_Building_Group" title="Shepherd Building Group">Shepherd Building Group</a> (who own <a href="/wiki/Portakabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Portakabin">Portakabin</a>), and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Portasilo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Portasilo (page does not exist)">Portasilo</a>, which makes <a href="/wiki/Bulk_material_handling" title="Bulk material handling">bulk handling</a> equipment such as <a href="/wiki/Silo" title="Silo">silos</a>, are in Huntington off the <a href="/wiki/A1036_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A1036 road">A1036</a> in the east of York; <a href="/wiki/AlphaGraphics" title="AlphaGraphics">AlphaGraphics UK</a> are next door (formerly in Seamer), and to <a href="/w/index.php?title=Monks_Cross&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Monks Cross (page does not exist)">Monks Cross</a> retail park. [London North Eastern Railways]] has its headquarters in York. <a href="/wiki/Terry%27s" title="Terry&#39;s">Terry's</a> chocolate was closed in September 2005 by its new owner <a href="/wiki/Kraft_Foods" title="Kraft Foods">Kraft Foods</a>, and production moved to Poland. <a href="/wiki/Costcutter" title="Costcutter">Costcutter</a> is based on the <a href="/wiki/A1079_road" title="A1079 road">A1079</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dunnington" title="Dunnington">Dunnington</a>. <a href="/wiki/Best_Western" title="Best Western">Best Western</a> Hotels UK are based at <a href="/wiki/Clifton_Without" title="Clifton Without">Clifton Without</a>. <a href="/wiki/CPP_Group" title="CPP Group">CPP Group</a> (credit card insurance) are on Holgate Park on the A59 in the north-west of the city centre; <a href="/wiki/Aviva" title="Aviva">Aviva</a> have a large site on Rougier Street (B1227) for equity release, life insurance, and pensions. <a href="/wiki/Rolawn" title="Rolawn">Rolawn</a> at the Laveracks Ind Est on the B1228 in <a href="/wiki/Elvington,_City_of_York" title="Elvington, City of York">Elvington</a> is Europe's largest producer of lawn turf, with its Medallion brand being the UK market leader. <a href="/wiki/DBS_National_Security_Vetting" title="DBS National Security Vetting">DBS National Security Vetting</a> is at Imphal Barracks in Fulford on the A19. <a href="/wiki/Tangerine_Confectionery" title="Tangerine Confectionery">Tangerine Confectionery</a> is off the A59, in Acomb Ings in the west of York, which makes toffee and fudge; its old site on <a href="/wiki/Coppergate_Shopping_Centre" title="Coppergate Shopping Centre">Coppergate</a> is now <a href="/wiki/Jorvik_Viking_Centre" title="Jorvik Viking Centre">Jorvik Viking Centre</a>; the neighbouring <a href="/wiki/British_Sugar" title="British Sugar">British Sugar</a> plant closed in 2007. <a href="/wiki/Sherbet_(powder)" title="Sherbet (powder)">Sherbet fountains</a> have been made in York since 1925; the brand was bought by Tangerine from Cadbury in 2008.
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_companies_in_Harrogate" title="List of companies in Harrogate">List of companies in Harrogate</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/WorldPay" class="mw-redirect" title="WorldPay">Streamline</a>, the UK's main <a href="/wiki/Merchant_account_provider" title="Merchant account provider">merchant account provider</a> formerly owned by <a href="/wiki/NatWest" title="NatWest">NatWest</a>, is on the B6162 at <a href="/wiki/Harlow_Hill,_Harrogate" class="mw-redirect" title="Harlow Hill, Harrogate">Harlow Hill</a> in the west of Harrogate; <a href="/wiki/Principal_Hotel_Company" title="Principal Hotel Company">Principal Hotel Company</a> UK (hotels), is at <a href="/wiki/Oatlands,_North_Yorkshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Oatlands, North Yorkshire">Oatlands</a> in the south of the town, where <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hein_Gericke&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hein Gericke (page does not exist)">Hein Gericke</a> UK is on Hornbeam Park, next to Harrogate College. <a href="/wiki/Dunlopillo" class="mw-redirect" title="Dunlopillo">Dunlopillo</a>, a world-leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Foam_rubber" title="Foam rubber">latex foam</a> mattresses was for many years off the A61 at <a href="/wiki/Pannal" title="Pannal">Pannal</a>, south of Harrogate, until 2003, and from 2008 has now been headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Huntingdon" title="Huntingdon">Huntingdon</a> (Cambs). The Canadian <a href="/wiki/McCain_Foods" title="McCain Foods">McCain Ltd</a> has been in <a href="/wiki/Scarborough,_North_Yorkshire" title="Scarborough, North Yorkshire">Scarborough</a> since 1969; <a href="/wiki/Legrand_(company)" title="Legrand (company)">Legrand</a> UK make <a href="/wiki/Cable_management" title="Cable management">cable management</a> systems at <a href="/wiki/Cayton" title="Cayton">Cayton</a> south of Scarborough on the B1261 next to McCain, and along the road from the coach builder <a href="/wiki/Plaxton" title="Plaxton">Plaxton</a>. <a href="/wiki/W_Boyes_%26_Co" class="mw-redirect" title="W Boyes &amp; Co">W Boyes &amp; Co</a> (retail) are in <a href="/wiki/Eastfield,_North_Yorkshire" title="Eastfield, North Yorkshire">Eastfield</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dale_Power_Solutions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dale Power Solutions (page does not exist)">Dale Power Solutions</a>, south of the B1261 on the Eastfield Ind Estate, make electrical power supply equipment. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Deep_Sea_Electronics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Deep Sea Electronics (page does not exist)">Deep Sea Electronics</a> make generator controllers on the <a href="/wiki/Hunmanby" title="Hunmanby">Hunmanby</a> Industrial Estate, off the <a href="/wiki/A165_road" title="A165 road">A165</a>, south of <a href="/wiki/Filey" title="Filey">Filey</a>. <a href="/wiki/Whitby_Seafoods_Ltd" title="Whitby Seafoods Ltd">Whitby Seafoods Ltd</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Whitby" title="Whitby">Whitby</a>; they are the biggest producer of <a href="/wiki/Scampi" title="Scampi">scampi</a> in the UK, and supply <a href="/wiki/Wetherspoons" title="Wetherspoons">Wetherspoons</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Westlers&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Westlers (page does not exist)">Westlers</a>, based on the B1257 in <a href="/wiki/Amotherby" title="Amotherby">Amotherby</a> make tinned convenience food, and the <a href="/wiki/Field_ration" title="Field ration">MoD's military ration packs</a> (also made by <a href="/wiki/Vestey_Group" title="Vestey Group">Vestey Foods</a> of <a href="/wiki/Coulsdon" title="Coulsdon">Coulsdon</a> in London). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalepak&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dalepak (page does not exist)">Dalepak</a> is based in <a href="/wiki/Leeming_Bar" title="Leeming Bar">Leeming Bar</a> which is owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=ABP_Food_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ABP Food Group (page does not exist)">ABP Food Group</a>; <a href="/wiki/Vale_of_Mowbray" title="Vale of Mowbray">Vale of Mowbray</a> have made pork pies in <a href="/wiki/Aiskew" title="Aiskew">Aiskew</a> since 1928. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Reed_Boardall&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reed Boardall (page does not exist)">Reed Boardall</a> have the UK's second largest cold storage site on the west side of the A1 at <a href="/wiki/Boroughbridge" title="Boroughbridge">Boroughbridge</a> (the largest is now in <a href="/wiki/Wisbech" title="Wisbech">Wisbech</a> in Cambridgeshire).
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg/220px-Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg/330px-Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg/440px-Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Theakston_Visitor_Centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_615591.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Theakston Visitor Centre in Masham</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/John_Smith%27s_Brewery" title="John Smith&#39;s Brewery">John Smith's Brewery</a> is at <a href="/wiki/Tadcaster" title="Tadcaster">Tadcaster</a>, owned by Heineken UK, which started brewing <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_Brown_Ale" title="Newcastle Brown Ale">Newcastle Brown Ale</a> in May 2010,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Smith_Brewery" class="mw-redirect" title="Samuel Smith Brewery">Samuel Smith Brewery</a>. At <a href="/wiki/Masham" title="Masham">Masham</a>, there is the <a href="/wiki/Theakston_Brewery" title="Theakston Brewery">Theakston Brewery</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Black_Sheep_Brewery" title="Black Sheep Brewery">Black Sheep Brewery</a>. Just to the north in <a href="/wiki/Aiskew" title="Aiskew">Aiskew</a>, <a href="/wiki/Masons_Gin" title="Masons Gin">Masons Gin</a> have a distillery.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Skipton_Building_Society" title="Skipton Building Society">Skipton Building Society</a> is in Skipton. <a href="/wiki/Silver_Cross_(company)" title="Silver Cross (company)">Silver Cross</a>, the iconic pram manufacturer named after Silver Cross Street in Leeds, is headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Broughton,_Craven" title="Broughton, Craven">Broughton</a> at the junction of the <a href="/wiki/A59_road" title="A59 road">A59</a> and <a href="/wiki/A56_road" title="A56 road">A56</a> west of Skipton, although its <i>Heritage</i> prams are made in <a href="/wiki/Bingley" title="Bingley">Bingley</a> (most are made overseas). Next to <a href="/wiki/Bentham_railway_station" title="Bentham railway station">Bentham railway station</a> (close to the Lancashire boundary) <a href="/wiki/Kidde" title="Kidde">Kidde</a> Products UK make <a href="/wiki/Fire_fighting_foam" class="mw-redirect" title="Fire fighting foam">foam</a> <a href="/wiki/Fire_extinguisher" title="Fire extinguisher">fire extinguishers</a>. <a href="/wiki/Quorn" title="Quorn">Quorn</a> is made in <a href="/wiki/Stokesley" title="Stokesley">Stokesley</a> by <a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Marlow Foods</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Rural_Payments_Agency" title="Rural Payments Agency">Rural Payments Agency</a> have a main office at Northallerton. <a href="/wiki/Econ_Engineering" title="Econ Engineering">Econ Engineering</a> on the A61 Ripon bypass near the B6265 roundabout are Britain's leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Winter_service_vehicle" title="Winter service vehicle">salt gritters</a>. <a href="/wiki/Severfield" title="Severfield">Severfield</a> is at Topcliffe on the east side of the <a href="/wiki/A168_road" title="A168 road">A168</a>, on a <a href="/wiki/RAF_Dalton" title="RAF Dalton">former airfield</a>; they built the Olympic International Broadcast Centre in London. At another <a href="/wiki/RAF_Marston_Moor" title="RAF Marston Moor">former airfield</a> at <a href="/wiki/Tockwith" title="Tockwith">Tockwith</a>, further south, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Stage_One_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Stage One (company) (page does not exist)">Stage One</a> built the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics_and_Paralympics_cauldron" title="2012 Summer Olympics and Paralympics cauldron">Olympic Cauldron</a>, the glowing Olympic Rings, and the aerial stage objects.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg/220px-Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg/330px-Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg/440px-Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2657" data-file-height="1772" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Optare_Manufacturing_Plant.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Optare bus factory in North Yorkshire, off the B1222</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Austin_Reed_(retailer)" title="Austin Reed (retailer)">Austin Reed</a>, who own <a href="/wiki/Viyella" title="Viyella">Viyella</a>, was on the A61 at the western end of <a href="/wiki/Thirsk_Racecourse" title="Thirsk Racecourse">Thirsk Racecourse</a> until 2016. <a href="/wiki/Slingsby_Aviation" title="Slingsby Aviation">Slingsby Aviation</a> make gliders and planes in <a href="/wiki/Kirkbymoorside" title="Kirkbymoorside">Kirkbymoorside</a>, on the <a href="/wiki/A170_road" title="A170 road">A170</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Perry_Slingsby_Systems&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Perry Slingsby Systems (page does not exist)">Perry Slingsby Systems</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Forum_Energy_Technologies" title="Forum Energy Technologies">Forum Energy Technologies</a>), next to Slingsby make <a href="/wiki/Remotely_operated_underwater_vehicle" title="Remotely operated underwater vehicle">remotely operated underwater vehicles</a> (ROVs), who have helped to develop the <a href="/wiki/NATO_Submarine_Rescue_System" title="NATO Submarine Rescue System">NATO Submarine Rescue System</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Karro_Food_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Karro Food Group (page does not exist)">Karro Food Group</a> based at Malton, are a pork processor, formerly part of <a href="/wiki/Vion_NV" title="Vion NV">Vion NV</a>. South of Selby, <a href="/wiki/Saint-Gobain" title="Saint-Gobain">Saint-Gobain</a> Glass UK (Solaglas) has made float glass for <a href="/wiki/Low_emissivity" title="Low emissivity">low emissivity</a> windows since 2000 next to the A19 at the A645 roundabout, directly south of the <a href="/wiki/Eggborough_power_station" title="Eggborough power station">Eggborough power station</a>. <a href="/wiki/Optare" title="Optare">Optare</a> make buses on a large industrial estate in <a href="/wiki/Sherburn-in-Elmet" class="mw-redirect" title="Sherburn-in-Elmet">Sherburn-in-Elmet</a> (previously in <a href="/wiki/Cross_Gates" title="Cross Gates">Cross Gates</a> in Leeds before May 2011), and have been part of <a href="/wiki/Hinduja_Group" title="Hinduja Group">Hinduja Group</a> since 2012.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="West_and_South">West and South</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_and_the_Humber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: West and South">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="box-More_citations_needed_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_and_the_Humber&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Leeds" title="Economy of Leeds">Economy of Leeds</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_companies_based_in_Leeds" title="List of companies based in Leeds">List of companies based in Leeds</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:ASDA_headquarters,_Great_Wilson_Street,_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg/220px-ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg/330px-ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg/440px-ASDA_headquarters%2C_Great_Wilson_Street%2C_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:ASDA_headquarters,_Great_Wilson_Street,_Leeds_-_geograph.org.uk_-_196141.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Asda's Headquarters, Asda House in <a href="/wiki/Leeds" title="Leeds">Leeds</a>; Asda was the UK's second largest supermarket until 2014, and is now third; Asda turned over £23.3bn in 2015, and is the region's largest company</div></div></div>
<p>Leeds is now a centre of financial services companies,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> with <a href="/wiki/Direct_Line" title="Direct Line">Direct Line</a><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/First_Direct" title="First Direct">First Direct</a><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> based there, as well as <a href="/wiki/Asda" title="Asda">Asda</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Arla_Foods_UK" title="Arla Foods UK">Arla Foods UK</a> (maker of <a href="/wiki/Lurpak" title="Lurpak">Lurpak</a> and Anchor butter) in <a href="/wiki/Stourton,_West_Yorkshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Stourton, West Yorkshire">Stourton</a> near the A639 junction 44 of the M1 (formerly in <a href="/wiki/Kirkstall" title="Kirkstall">Kirkstall</a> near Yorkshire Television). The <a href="/wiki/Green_Flag" title="Green Flag">Green Flag</a> roadside recovery firm has its main call centre (in <a href="/wiki/Farsley" title="Farsley">Farsley</a>). <a href="/wiki/HSBC" title="HSBC">HSBC</a> opened their first UK call centre in the city, taking advantage of its advanced communications network which also led to the founding of <a href="/wiki/Freeserve" title="Freeserve">Freeserve</a> in Leeds. The <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Health_(United_Kingdom)" class="mw-redirect" title="Department of Health (United Kingdom)">Department of Health</a> has a large administration operation at <a href="/wiki/Quarry_Hill,_Leeds" title="Quarry Hill, Leeds">Quarry House</a>, a local landmark. The <a href="/wiki/Child_Maintenance_and_Enforcement_Commission" title="Child Maintenance and Enforcement Commission">Child Maintenance and Enforcement Commission</a> was at <a href="/w/index.php?title=One_Leeds_City_Office_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="One Leeds City Office Park (page does not exist)">One Leeds City Office Park</a> until 2012, off the A653 south of Bridgewater Place. The <a href="/wiki/NHS_Appointments_Commission" class="mw-redirect" title="NHS Appointments Commission">NHS Appointments Commission</a> and former <a href="/wiki/Strategic_health_authority" title="Strategic health authority">NHS Yorkshire and the Humber</a> were next to the north side of the A65 at the A58(M) junction near the former <a href="/wiki/Park_Lane_College" class="mw-redirect" title="Park Lane College">Park Lane College</a>, where further east along the A58 is the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Callcredit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Callcredit (page does not exist)">Callcredit</a> credit reference agency, and on the opposite side of the inner ring-road from the <a href="/wiki/Skills_for_Care" title="Skills for Care">Skills for Care</a> <a href="/wiki/Sector_Skills_Councils" class="mw-redirect" title="Sector Skills Councils">sector skills council</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Waddingtons" title="Waddingtons">Waddingtons</a> board game company was founded in Leeds, as was the Burton tailoring company (the Burton Group became the <a href="/wiki/Arcadia_Group" title="Arcadia Group">Arcadia Group</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Marks_%26_Spencer" title="Marks &amp; Spencer">M &amp; S</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Tetley%27s_Brewery" title="Tetley&#39;s Brewery">Tetley's Brewery</a> closed in 2011 and moved operations to Northampton (<a href="/wiki/Carlsberg_Group" title="Carlsberg Group">Carlsberg</a>). <a href="/wiki/Aramark" title="Aramark">Aramark UK</a> is in <a href="/wiki/West_Park,_Leeds" title="West Park, Leeds">West Park, Leeds</a>, in the north of the city, off the <a href="/wiki/Leeds_Outer_Ring_Road" title="Leeds Outer Ring Road">ring road</a>.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/British_Library" title="British Library">British Library</a> is sited at <a href="/wiki/Thorp_Arch,_West_Yorkshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Thorp Arch, West Yorkshire">Thorpe Arch</a> near <a href="/wiki/Wetherby" title="Wetherby">Wetherby</a>, home of <a href="/wiki/Goldenfry" title="Goldenfry">Goldenfry</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dr._Oetker" title="Dr. Oetker">Dr. Oetker</a> products are made at <a href="/wiki/Colton,_Leeds" title="Colton, Leeds">Colton</a> near M1 junction 46 and <a href="/wiki/Sherburn-in-Elmet" class="mw-redirect" title="Sherburn-in-Elmet">Sherburn-in-Elmet</a>; at Thorpe Park Business Park in the east of Leeds (<a href="/wiki/Austhorpe" title="Austhorpe">Austhorpe</a>) also is <a href="/wiki/Northern_Gas_Networks" title="Northern Gas Networks">Northern Gas Networks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Republic_(retailer)" title="Republic (retailer)">Republic (retailer)</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ellie_Louise&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ellie Louise (page does not exist)">Ellie Louise</a>, a clothes retailer, is at <a href="/wiki/Sturton_Grange" title="Sturton Grange">Sturton Grange</a> north of Garforth on the A642, south of M1 junction 47 on the Helios 47 Ind Estate, near <a href="/wiki/Ginetta_Cars" title="Ginetta Cars">Ginetta Cars</a>. <a href="/wiki/Unilever_Leeds" title="Unilever Leeds">Unilever Leeds</a> (former Gibbs Proprietaries from 1965, then Elida Gibbs from 1971, then <a href="/w/index.php?title=Elida_Faberg%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Elida Fabergé (page does not exist)">Elida Fabergé</a>) have their aerosol division at <a href="/wiki/Whinmoor" title="Whinmoor">Whinmoor</a>, in north-east Leeds, administrated by <a href="/wiki/Faberg%C3%A9_(cosmetics)" title="Fabergé (cosmetics)">Lever Fabergé</a>. It claims to be the largest aerosol factory in the world, and has their research centre, and makes <a href="/wiki/Impulse_(body_mist)" title="Impulse (body mist)">Impulse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Axe_(grooming_product)" class="mw-redirect" title="Axe (grooming product)">Lynx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dove_(personal_care_product_brand)" class="mw-redirect" title="Dove (personal care product brand)">Dove</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sure_(brand)" class="mw-redirect" title="Sure (brand)">Sure</a>. <a href="/wiki/Agfa-Gevaert" title="Agfa-Gevaert">Agfa Graphics</a> (Belgian) have their only UK factory next to Fabergé in Whinmoor, making <a href="/wiki/Computer_to_plate" title="Computer to plate">computer to plate</a> <a href="/wiki/Offset_printing" title="Offset printing">offset printers</a>; 85% of the world's banknotes are printed with the parent company's technology. Nearby in Seacroft is <a href="/wiki/Komori" title="Komori">Komori</a> UK (printing presses).
</p><p>Symington's make breakfast cereals on the Thornes Farm Business Park, near the <a href="/wiki/A63_road" title="A63 road">A63</a> (M1 junction 45). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Daniels_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Daniels Group (page does not exist)">Daniels Group</a>, makers of <a href="/w/index.php?title=New_Covent_Garden_Food_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="New Covent Garden Food Company (page does not exist)">New Covent Garden Food Company</a> soups (made on the <a href="/wiki/Europarc,_Grimsby" class="mw-redirect" title="Europarc, Grimsby">Europarc, Grimsby</a>), are on the Acorn Business Park, off the <a href="/wiki/A64_road" title="A64 road">A64</a>, next to the Asda at <a href="/wiki/Killingbeck" title="Killingbeck">Killingbeck</a>. <a href="/wiki/Sound_Leisure" title="Sound Leisure">Sound Leisure</a> is the UK's leading manufacturer of juke boxes. <a href="/wiki/WABCO_Vehicle_Control_Systems" title="WABCO Vehicle Control Systems">WABCO Vehicle Control Systems</a> UK (air brakes) is in <a href="/wiki/Morley,_West_Yorkshire" title="Morley, West Yorkshire">Morley</a>, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=QHotels&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="QHotels (page does not exist)">QHotels</a> are on <i>Bruntcliffe Road</i> (A650) in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bruntcliffe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bruntcliffe (page does not exist)">Bruntcliffe</a>. East of Morley off the A6110 is <a href="/wiki/DePuy" title="DePuy">DePuy International</a> (orthopaedics). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hermes_Logistik_Gruppe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hermes Logistik Gruppe (page does not exist)">Hermes Europe</a> (former Parcelnet before 2009, which was Directline and Speedlink before 1999), based at Capitol Park on the A650 at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Topcliffe,_West_Yorkshire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Topcliffe, West Yorkshire (page does not exist)">Topcliffe</a>, is the UK's largest home delivery company, and is part of Grattan's parent company. ATB Morley, on the B6157 next to the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Owlcotes_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Owlcotes Centre (page does not exist)">Owlcotes Centre</a> and owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Antriebstechnik&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Antriebstechnik (page does not exist)">Antriebstechnik</a> AG, make electric motors. Further along the B6157 from ATB Morley at the junction with B6155, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hainsworth&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hainsworth (page does not exist)">Hainsworth</a> makes speciality textiles such as military uniforms and in 1975 produced the first <a href="/wiki/Nomex" title="Nomex">Nomex</a> flame-retardant <a href="/wiki/Flight_suit" title="Flight suit">flight suits</a> for <a href="/wiki/Jet_aircraft" title="Jet aircraft">fast-jet</a> pilots in the UK; their TITAN outfit is used by <a href="/wiki/Riot_police" title="Riot police">riot police</a> and firefighters, with ceremonial fabrics made from <a href="/wiki/Worsted" title="Worsted">worsted</a> <a href="/wiki/Barathea" title="Barathea">barathea</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peaked_cap" title="Peaked cap">uniform caps</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Household_Division" title="Household Division">Household Division</a>, and uniforms for others such as <a href="/wiki/London_Underground" title="London Underground">London Underground</a>. <a href="/wiki/Clariant" title="Clariant">Clariant UK</a>, the chemical company, was in <a href="/wiki/Yeadon,_West_Yorkshire" title="Yeadon, West Yorkshire">Yeadon</a>, with a factory in <a href="/wiki/Horsforth" title="Horsforth">Horsforth</a>; <a href="/wiki/Brenntag" title="Brenntag">Brenntag</a> UK is based at the A65/A658 junction at Rawdon Park in Yeadon (former Albion Chemicals before 2006) next to the fire station.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/EMIS_Health" title="EMIS Health">EMIS Health</a> are off the A658 in central Yeadon, and are a main supplier of GP computer systems. Craftsman Tools on the A659 in Otley make <a href="/w/index.php?title=Toolholding&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Toolholding (page does not exist)">toolholding</a> systems and <a href="/wiki/Fixture_(tool)" title="Fixture (tool)">fixtures</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sinclairs&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sinclairs (page does not exist)">Sinclairs</a> make the <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Silvine&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Silvine (page does not exist)">Silvine</a></i> brand of stationery at Otley. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Allied_Glass&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Allied Glass (page does not exist)">Allied Glass</a> based in south Leeds at the A61/A639 junction, and also has a main plant at Knottingley east of town on the A645, makes glass bottles for whisky. Toggi outdoor clothing (equestrian) is at Confederation Park at the M621 junction 2 with the A643, and with Champion who make riding hats and body protectors; <a href="/wiki/George_Cohen,_Sons_and_Company" title="George Cohen, Sons and Company">600 Group</a>, based near junction 2 of the M621, are the world's biggest manufacturer of manual and CNC lathes; it makes <a href="/w/index.php?title=Colchester-Harrison&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Colchester-Harrison (page does not exist)">Colchester-Harrison</a> lathes, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Pratt_Burnerd_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Pratt Burnerd International (page does not exist)">Pratt Burnerd International</a> <a href="/wiki/Chuck_(engineering)" title="Chuck (engineering)">lathe-chucks</a> with a lathe factory at Heckmondwike. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Oliver_Douglas_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Oliver Douglas (company) (page does not exist)">Oliver Douglas</a>, on the Tong Road Ind Estate off the B6154 in Wortley, make industrial (catering) washing machines. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Perry_Uniform&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Perry Uniform (page does not exist)">Perry Uniform</a> makes many school uniforms for many <a href="/wiki/Independent_school_(United_Kingdom)" title="Independent school (United Kingdom)">independent schools</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/Caldervale_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Caldervale Line">railway</a> off the B6154 in Upper Armley. <a href="/wiki/Sulzer_(manufacturer)" title="Sulzer (manufacturer)">Sulzer Pumps</a> UK have a large manufacturing facility on the <a href="/wiki/Leeds_Outer_Ring_Road" title="Leeds Outer Ring Road">A6110</a> near the <a href="/wiki/A643_road" title="A643 road">A643</a> roundabout. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Pland_Stainless&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Pland Stainless (page does not exist)">Pland Stainless</a> make large sinks for laboratories and hospitals. Leeds is the second largest manufacturing city in the UK, after London.
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_companies_based_in_Bradford" title="List of companies based in Bradford">List of companies based in Bradford</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Morrisons" title="Morrisons">Morrisons</a> is based in Bradford; it has 132,000 staff and opened its first supermarket in 1961 in a converted cinema; it turned over £17.6bn in 2015, and is the region's second largest company. Also in Bradford are <a href="/wiki/Club_18-30" title="Club 18-30">Club 18-30</a>, <a href="/wiki/Provident_Financial" title="Provident Financial">Provident Financial</a>, <a href="/wiki/Seabrook_Potato_Crisps" title="Seabrook Potato Crisps">Seabrook Potato Crisps</a>, <a href="/wiki/Safestyle_UK" title="Safestyle UK">Safestyle UK</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Building_Society" title="Yorkshire Building Society">Yorkshire Building Society</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barratts_Shoes" title="Barratts Shoes">Stylo</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Grattan_plc" title="Grattan plc">Grattan</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Otto_GmbH" title="Otto GmbH">Otto GmbH</a> since 2000)<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> catalogue retailer, and <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Water" title="Yorkshire Water">Yorkshire Water</a>. <a href="/wiki/Santander_UK" title="Santander UK">Santander UK</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Abbey_National" title="Abbey National">Abbey</a>) has its <a href="/wiki/Savings_account" title="Savings account">savings</a> division there. The <a href="/wiki/Halifax_(United_Kingdom_bank)" class="mw-redirect" title="Halifax (United Kingdom bank)">Halifax</a> bank (former Building Society) is based in Halifax, the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Bank" title="Yorkshire Bank">Yorkshire Bank</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/CYBG_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="CYBG plc">CYBG plc</a> and the <a href="/wiki/National_Australia_Bank" title="National Australia Bank">National Australia Bank</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Leeds_Building_Society" title="Leeds Building Society">Leeds Building Society</a> in Leeds, and with <a href="/wiki/UK_Asset_Resolution" title="UK Asset Resolution">UK Asset Resolution</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Bradford_%26_Bingley" title="Bradford &amp; Bingley">Bradford &amp; Bingley</a>) and <a href="/wiki/NRAM_Limited" class="mw-redirect" title="NRAM Limited">NRAM Limited</a> (former Northern Rock) in <a href="/wiki/Crossflatts" title="Crossflatts">Crossflatts</a>. The area between Leeds, Bradford and Wakefield is known as the <a href="/wiki/Rhubarb_Triangle" title="Rhubarb Triangle">Rhubarb Triangle</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg/220px-Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="107" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg/330px-Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg/440px-Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="310" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hallmark_Cards_-_Dawson_Lane_-_geograph.org.uk_-_445059.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Hallmark_Cards" title="Hallmark Cards">Hallmark Cards UK</a> factory off the A650 (Tong Street), the view on Dawson Lane</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Empire_Stores&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Empire Stores (page does not exist)">Empire Stores</a> of Bradford was Britain's first <a href="/wiki/Mail_order" title="Mail order">mail order</a> firm in 1890, bought by <a href="/wiki/Redcats" title="Redcats">Redcats</a> UK (French) and closed in 2009; it is now the site of Redcats UK in the north of the town centre. BASF Performance Products (<a href="/wiki/Ciba_Specialty_Chemicals" title="Ciba Specialty Chemicals">Ciba Specialty Chemicals</a> until 2008, then Allied Colloids before 1997) is in <a href="/wiki/Low_Moor,_Bradford" title="Low Moor, Bradford">Low Moor</a>; it makes many chemicals including <a href="/wiki/Thickening_agent" title="Thickening agent">thickening agents</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bowers_Metrology_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bowers Metrology Group (page does not exist)">Bowers Metrology Group</a>, on the B6381 near the junction with <a href="/wiki/A6177_road" title="A6177 road">A6177</a> at <a href="/wiki/Bradford_Moor" title="Bradford Moor">Bradford Moor</a>, are a leading measuring instruments company, and part of Spear &amp; Jackson. <a href="/wiki/Equifax" title="Equifax">Equifax</a> is off the A650 in central Bradford, opposite the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Leisure_Exchange&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Leisure Exchange (page does not exist)">Leisure Exchange</a>; next door <a href="/wiki/Royal_Bank_of_Scotland_Group" title="Royal Bank of Scotland Group">RBS Group</a> have a call centre. <a href="/wiki/Federal-Mogul" title="Federal-Mogul">Federal-Mogul</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A650_road" title="A650 road">A650</a> in east Bradford, makes automotive parts (<a href="/wiki/Gudgeon_pin" title="Gudgeon pin">gudgeon pins</a> and <a href="/wiki/Piston" title="Piston">pistons</a>). <a href="/wiki/Princes_(company)" class="mw-redirect" title="Princes (company)">Princes Soft Drinks</a> have their main factory south of the A650 at <a href="/wiki/Tong_(ward)" title="Tong (ward)">Tong Street</a>; <a href="/wiki/Next_plc" title="Next plc">Next</a> have a large warehouse nearby.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/BorgWarner" title="BorgWarner">BorgWarner</a> Turbo Systems make automotive <a href="/wiki/Turbocharger" title="Turbocharger">turbochargers</a> (including <a href="/wiki/Variable-geometry_turbocharger" title="Variable-geometry turbocharger">variable-geometry turbochargers</a>) on the Euroway Ind Est off the M606, and produces around 750,000 a year; <a href="/wiki/Jacuzzi" title="Jacuzzi">Jacuzzi UK</a> is nearby. Knightsbridge Furniture is on the <a href="/wiki/B6165_road" class="mw-redirect" title="B6165 road">B6165</a> in Lister Hills. <a href="/wiki/Nufarm" title="Nufarm">Nufarm</a> UK (<a href="/w/index.php?title=A_H_Marks&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="A H Marks (page does not exist)">A H Marks</a> before 2008), make chemicals for <a href="/wiki/Phenoxy_herbicide" title="Phenoxy herbicide">phenoxy herbicides</a>, between <a href="/wiki/Wyke" title="Wyke">Wyke</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oakenshaw,_West_Yorkshire" title="Oakenshaw, West Yorkshire">Oakenshaw</a>. <a href="/wiki/Hield" title="Hield">Hield</a> (luxury clothing) is in <a href="/wiki/Trident,_West_Yorkshire" title="Trident, West Yorkshire">Trident</a> parish, south of the city centre. <a href="/wiki/Pace_plc" title="Pace plc">Pace plc</a> (owned since 2016 by <a href="/wiki/Arris_International" title="Arris International">Arris International</a>) in <a href="/wiki/Saltaire" title="Saltaire">Saltaire</a> is the global market leader in <a href="/wiki/Set-top_box" title="Set-top box">set-top boxes</a>; Pace bought part of <a href="/wiki/Acorn_Computers" title="Acorn Computers">Acorn</a>, and based its set top boxes on the <a href="/wiki/RISC_OS" title="RISC OS">RISC OS</a>, which it owned. <a href="/wiki/Denso" title="Denso">Denso Marston Ltd</a> make <a href="/wiki/Radiator_(engine_cooling)" title="Radiator (engine cooling)">car radiators</a> in <a href="/wiki/Shipley,_West_Yorkshire" title="Shipley, West Yorkshire">Shipley</a>; HMRC (former Inland Revenue) have their main national payments office (<a href="/w/index.php?title=HMRC_Accounts_Office&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HMRC Accounts Office (page does not exist)">HMRC Accounts Office</a>) between the River Aire and the Leeds Liverpool canal at Shipley, opposite Salt's Mill, in a hexagonal building; <a href="/w/index.php?title=CarnaudMetalbox_Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="CarnaudMetalbox Engineering (page does not exist)">CarnaudMetalbox Engineering</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Crown_Holdings" title="Crown Holdings">Crown Holdings</a>) are based off the <a href="/wiki/A6038_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A6038 road">A6038</a>, and make metal <a href="/wiki/Canning" title="Canning">canning</a> machines. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Anetic_Aid&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Anetic Aid (page does not exist)">Anetic Aid</a> is on Baildon Business Park on the A6038, and make <a href="/wiki/Operating_theater" title="Operating theater">operating theatre</a> equipment (in Portsmouth). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Brook_Taverner&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Brook Taverner (page does not exist)">Brook Taverner</a> is Europe's largest corporate clothing supplier in <a href="/wiki/Ingrow" title="Ingrow">Ingrow</a>, off the A629. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cinetic_Landis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cinetic Landis (page does not exist)">Cinetic Landis</a> UK, at <a href="/wiki/Cross_Hills" title="Cross Hills">Cross Hills</a> on the B6265, make CNC-controlled <a href="/wiki/Grinding_machine" title="Grinding machine">grinding machines</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Reflecting_Roadstuds_Ltd" title="Reflecting Roadstuds Ltd">Reflecting Roadstuds Ltd</a>, where <a href="/wiki/Cat%27s_eye_(road)" title="Cat&#39;s eye (road)">cat's eyes</a> were invented by <a href="/wiki/Percy_Shaw" title="Percy Shaw">Percy Shaw</a>, are in <a href="/wiki/Boothtown" title="Boothtown">Boothtown</a>, in the north of Halifax. <a href="/wiki/Rhodia_(company)" title="Rhodia (company)">Rhodia</a> Novecare UK are at <a href="/wiki/Holywell_Green" title="Holywell Green">Holywell Green</a>, south of Halifax, and make <a href="/wiki/Surfactant" title="Surfactant">surfactants</a> for cosmetics; to the north <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sia_Abrasives&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sia Abrasives (page does not exist)">sia Fibral</a> make <a href="/wiki/Nonwoven_fabric" title="Nonwoven fabric">non-woven</a> abrasives at <a href="/wiki/Greetland" title="Greetland">Greetland</a> off the B6114 (which leads to the <a href="/wiki/Scammonden_Bridge" title="Scammonden Bridge">Scammonden Bridge</a>) with the company's UK HQ in Brighouse. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gower_Furniture&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gower Furniture (page does not exist)">Gower Furniture</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Nobia" title="Nobia">Nobia</a>) is north-east of Halifax in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Holmfield&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Holmfield (page does not exist)">Holmfield</a> in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bradshaw,_West_Yorkshire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bradshaw, West Yorkshire (page does not exist)">Bradshaw</a>. <a href="/wiki/McVitie%27s" title="McVitie&#39;s">McVitie's</a> Cake Company (Jamaica Ginger and <a href="/wiki/Golden_syrup" title="Golden syrup">Lyle's Golden Syrup</a> cakes, and <a href="/wiki/Hobnob_biscuit" title="Hobnob biscuit">HobNob</a> <a href="/wiki/Flapjack_(oat_bar)" title="Flapjack (oat bar)">flapjacks</a>) is in west Halifax. <a href="/wiki/Timeform" title="Timeform">Timeform</a> (horse <a href="/wiki/Racecard" title="Racecard">racecards</a>) are near the A58/A629 roundabout in the north of the town centre and the A58 bridge over <a href="/wiki/Hebble_Brook" title="Hebble Brook">Hebble Brook</a>. Crosslee plc, south of <a href="/wiki/Hipperholme" title="Hipperholme">Hipperholme</a> on the A644 towards <a href="/wiki/Brighouse" title="Brighouse">Brighouse</a>, is Europe's largest independent <a href="/wiki/Tumble_dryer" class="mw-redirect" title="Tumble dryer">tumble dryer</a> manufacturer, under the <i>White Knight</i> brand. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Calrec_Audio&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Calrec Audio (page does not exist)">Calrec Audio</a>, an electronics firm that makes <a href="/wiki/Mixing_console" title="Mixing console">mixing desks</a>, are on the <a href="/wiki/A6033_road_(Great_Britain)" class="mw-redirect" title="A6033 road (Great Britain)">A6033</a> at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Nutclough&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nutclough (page does not exist)">Nutclough</a>, Hebden Bridge. <a href="/wiki/Cressi-Sub" title="Cressi-Sub">Cressi-Sub</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Scuba_set" title="Scuba set">scuba gear</a>) are at Atlas Mill, Brighouse; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Kent_Introl&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Kent Introl (page does not exist)">Kent Introl</a> (control valves) are in the east of Brighouse off the <a href="/wiki/A644_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A644 road">A644</a>. Bedford Shelving are to the west. <a href="/wiki/Marshalls_plc" title="Marshalls plc">Marshalls plc</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pavement_(architecture)" title="Pavement (architecture)">paving stones</a>) are next to the River Calder in <a href="/wiki/Elland" title="Elland">Elland</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Arran_Isle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Arran Isle (page does not exist)">Arran Isle</a> (hardware), near <a href="/wiki/Suma_(co-operative)" title="Suma (co-operative)">Suma Foods</a>. <a href="/wiki/Terberg_Group" title="Terberg Group">Terberg</a> DTS UK, supply its own <a href="/w/index.php?title=Distribution_tractor&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Distribution tractor (page does not exist)">distribution tractors</a> and <a href="/wiki/Schopf" title="Schopf">Schopf</a> aircraft tow tractors from Lowfields Business Park, next to the River Calder off the <a href="/wiki/A629_road" title="A629 road">A629</a> in <a href="/wiki/Elland" title="Elland">Elland</a>; nearby <a href="/wiki/Weir_Group" title="Weir Group">Weir Power &amp; Industrial</a> make Hopkinson and Batley brands of valves.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Fox%27s_Biscuits" title="Fox&#39;s Biscuits">Fox's Biscuits</a> (part of Northern Foods) and <a href="/wiki/Cattles" title="Cattles">Cattles</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Batley" title="Batley">Batley</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=HSL_Manufacturing&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HSL Manufacturing (page does not exist)">HSL Manufacturing</a> (High Seat Ltd) are on Grange Road Ind Est (B6128) in the east of Batley, north of <a href="/wiki/Hanging_Heaton" title="Hanging Heaton">Hanging Heaton</a>. <a href="/wiki/Rohm_and_Haas" title="Rohm and Haas">Rohm and Haas</a> UK (former Morton International, making chemicals) is on the B6117 in <a href="/wiki/Dewsbury_Moor" title="Dewsbury Moor">Dewsbury Moor</a>, on the south edge of Heckmondwike. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Birkby%E2%80%99s_Plastics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Birkby’s Plastics (page does not exist)">Birkby’s Plastics</a> make automotive components in <a href="/wiki/Liversedge" title="Liversedge">Liversedge</a>, and was the first company in the UK to mould plastic in the First World War. <a href="/wiki/Rieter" title="Rieter">Rieter Automotive</a> make car furnishings on the <a href="/wiki/A638_road" title="A638 road">A638</a> in <a href="/wiki/Heckmondwike" title="Heckmondwike">Heckmondwike</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=TMD_Friction&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="TMD Friction (page does not exist)">TMD Friction</a> make <a href="/wiki/Brake_pad" title="Brake pad">brake pads</a> (Mintex  part of BBA) off the A638 at <a href="/wiki/Chain_Bar_junction" class="mw-redirect" title="Chain Bar junction">Chain Bar</a>, Cleckheaton;
