<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_media">Local media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_and_the_Humber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Local media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:BBC_buildings,_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg/220px-BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg/330px-BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg/440px-BBC_buildings%2C_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1536" data-file-height="2048" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:BBC_buildings,_Kingston_upon_Hull.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>BBC in <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Gardens,_Hull" title="Queen&#39;s Gardens, Hull">Queen's Gardens, Hull</a></div></div></div>
<ul><li>Local BBC Television comes from <a href="/wiki/BBC_Look_North_(Yorkshire_and_North_Midlands)" title="BBC Look North (Yorkshire and North Midlands)"><i>BBC Look North</i> in Leeds</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Look_North_(East_Yorkshire_and_Lincolnshire)" title="BBC Look North (East Yorkshire and Lincolnshire)"><i>BBC Look North</i> in Hull</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Look_North_(North_East_and_Cumbria)" title="BBC Look North (North East and Cumbria)"><i>BBC Look North</i> in Newcastle</a> and <a href="/wiki/BBC_North_West_Tonight" title="BBC North West Tonight">BBC North West Tonight</a> in <a href="/wiki/Salford,_Greater_Manchester" class="mw-redirect" title="Salford, Greater Manchester">Salford</a>. <a href="/wiki/ITV_Yorkshire" title="ITV Yorkshire">ITV Yorkshire</a> is on <i>Kirkstall Road</i> to the west of Leeds city centre, which broadcasts <i><a href="/wiki/ITV_News_Calendar" class="mw-redirect" title="ITV News Calendar">Calendar</a></i> and some national programming. <a href="/wiki/ITV_Granada" title="ITV Granada">ITV Granada</a> and <a href="/wiki/ITV_Tyne_Tees" title="ITV Tyne Tees">ITV Tyne Tees</a> also cover parts of the region. <a href="/wiki/Digital_switchover_dates_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Digital switchover dates in the United Kingdom">Digital switchover</a> took place in August 2011 for most of the region, with <a href="/wiki/Emley_Moor_transmitting_station" title="Emley Moor transmitting station">Emley Moor</a> (the main TV transmitter for West and South Yorkshire) converting to <a href="/wiki/Digital_terrestrial_television_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Digital terrestrial television in the United Kingdom">digital</a> in mid-September. Emley Moor is the tallest free-standing structure in the UK, and the 25th <a href="/wiki/List_of_tallest_towers_in_the_world" class="mw-redirect" title="List of tallest towers in the world">tallest in the world</a>, and was designed by <a href="/wiki/Ove_Arup" title="Ove Arup">Ove Arup</a>. The original tower famously collapsed in March 1969.</li>
<li>BBC Radios <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Humberside" title="BBC Radio Humberside">Humberside</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Leeds" title="BBC Radio Leeds">Leeds</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Sheffield" title="BBC Radio Sheffield">Sheffield</a> and <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_York" title="BBC Radio York">York</a>. Radio Humberside's <a href="/wiki/High_Hunsley" title="High Hunsley">High Hunsley</a> transmitter covers most of the region, and beyond.</li>
<li>Local commercial stations include <a href="/wiki/Dearne_FM" title="Dearne FM">Dearne FM</a> (Barnsley), <a href="/wiki/The_Pulse_of_West_Yorkshire" class="mw-redirect" title="The Pulse of West Yorkshire">The Pulse of West Yorkshire</a> (Bradford), <a href="/wiki/Trax_FM" title="Trax FM">Trax FM</a> (Doncaster), <a href="/wiki/Compass_FM" title="Compass FM">Compass FM</a> (Grimsby), <a href="/wiki/Stray_FM" title="Stray FM">97.2 Stray FM</a> (Harrogate), <a href="/wiki/Pennine_FM" title="Pennine FM">Home 107.9</a> (Huddersfield), <a href="/wiki/96.9_Viking_FM" class="mw-redirect" title="96.9 Viking FM">96.9 Viking FM</a> (Hull), <a href="/wiki/Rother_FM" title="Rother FM">Rother FM</a>, <a href="/wiki/96.3_Radio_Aire" class="mw-redirect" title="96.3 Radio Aire">96.3 Radio Aire</a> (Leeds), <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Coast_Radio" title="Yorkshire Coast Radio">Yorkshire Coast Radio</a> (<a href="/wiki/Scarborough,_North_Yorkshire" title="Scarborough, North Yorkshire">Scarborough</a>/<a href="/wiki/Whitby" title="Whitby">Whitby</a>/<a href="/wiki/Bridlington" title="Bridlington">Bridlington</a>), <a href="/wiki/Hallam_FM" title="Hallam FM">Hallam FM</a> (Sheffield), <a href="/wiki/Fresh_Radio" title="Fresh Radio">Fresh Radio</a> (<a href="/wiki/Skipton" title="Skipton">Skipton</a>), <a href="/wiki/Real_Radio_(Yorkshire)" class="mw-redirect" title="Real Radio (Yorkshire)">Real Radio</a> (<a href="/wiki/Tingley" title="Tingley">Tingley</a>), <a href="/wiki/Ridings_FM" title="Ridings FM">Ridings FM</a> (Wakefield), <a href="/wiki/Capital_Yorkshire" title="Capital Yorkshire">Capital Yorkshire</a> (formerly Galaxy Yorkshire), <a href="/wiki/Minster_FM" title="Minster FM">Minster FM</a> (York) and 107.8 Beverley FM.</li>
<li>National radio is broadcast from <a href="/wiki/Belmont_transmitting_station" title="Belmont transmitting station">Belmont</a> in the south-east, <a href="/wiki/Bilsdale_transmitting_station" title="Bilsdale transmitting station">Bilsdale</a> for North Yorkshire, and <a href="/wiki/Holme_Moss" title="Holme Moss">Holme Moss</a> for South and West Yorkshire. <a href="/wiki/Moorside_Edge_transmitting_station" title="Moorside Edge transmitting station">Moorside Edge</a> east of <a href="/wiki/Scammonden_Reservoir" title="Scammonden Reservoir">Scammonden Water</a> near the M62 is a main <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live" title="BBC Radio 5 Live">5 Live</a> transmitter on 909MW.</li>
<li>Local newspapers are the <i><a href="/wiki/Bradford_Telegraph_and_Argus" class="mw-redirect" title="Bradford Telegraph and Argus">Bradford Telegraph and Argus</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Evening_Courier" class="mw-redirect" title="Evening Courier">Evening Courier</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Grimsby_Telegraph" title="Grimsby Telegraph">Grimsby Telegraph</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Huddersfield_Examiner" class="mw-redirect" title="Huddersfield Examiner">Huddersfield Examiner</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Hull_Daily_Mail" title="Hull Daily Mail">Hull Daily Mail</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Scarborough_Evening_News" class="mw-redirect" title="Scarborough Evening News">Scarborough Evening News</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Scunthorpe_Telegraph" title="Scunthorpe Telegraph">Scunthorpe Telegraph</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Sheffield_Star" title="Sheffield Star">Sheffield Star</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Press_(York)" title="The Press (York)">The Press (York)</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Wakefield_Express" title="Wakefield Express">Wakefield Express</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Evening_Post" title="Yorkshire Evening Post">Yorkshire Evening Post</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Post" class="mw-redirect" title="Yorkshire Post">Yorkshire Post</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Polestar Petty in central Leeds, with <a href="/wiki/Offset_printing" title="Offset printing">web offset</a>, for many years printed <i><a href="/wiki/TVTimes" title="TVTimes">TVTimes</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Radio_Times" title="Radio Times">Radio Times</a></i>, and many colour supplements, including the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mail" title="Daily Mail">Daily Mail</a></i> weekend magazine, but closed in December 2014. <a href="/wiki/RR_Donnelley" title="RR Donnelley">RR Donnelley UK Directory</a> of <a href="/wiki/Flaxby" title="Flaxby">Flaxby</a> Moor, south of the A59 east of A1(M) junction 47, printed the <i><a href="/wiki/Yellow_pages" title="Yellow pages">Yellow Pages</a></i>, until the site closed at the end of 2015. Polestar Chantry, off the A650 on the Wakefield 41 estate, prints <i><a href="/wiki/Marie_Claire" title="Marie Claire">Marie Claire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Good_Housekeeping" title="Good Housekeeping">Good Housekeeping</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Woman%27s_Weekly_(UK_magazine)" title="Woman&#39;s Weekly (UK magazine)">Woman's Weekly</a></i>, <i>Real Life</i>, <i><a href="/wiki/BBC_Good_Food" title="BBC Good Food">BBC Good Food</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/BBC_Gardeners%27_World" title="BBC Gardeners&#39; World">BBC Gardeners' World</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Prima_(magazine)" title="Prima (magazine)">Prima</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Woman_%26_Home" title="Woman &amp; Home">Woman &amp; Home</a></i>, <i>Red</i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Country_Life_(magazine)" title="Country Life (magazine)">Country Life</a></i>. Polestar Sheffield prints the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Telegraph" class="mw-redirect" title="Daily Telegraph">Telegraph</a></i> magazine, and <i><a href="/wiki/Hello!" class="mw-redirect" title="Hello!">Hello!</a></i>.</li>
<li>Yorkshire and Humberside are very supportive in their approach to theatre and performance festivals and hold regional championships for young performers every 2 years. The championship is sectioned in Dance, Music and Speech &amp; Drama. The most recent championship was held on Saturday 8 September, at St Margaret's Church Hall, Horsforth in Leeds. Helen Wilson, of Harrogate, titled Music Champion and with 17-year-old Lee Peart, of Cleethorpes, winning the Speech &amp; Drama championship.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
